                END;

  CODE
  {
    VAR
      GLSetup@1100529613 : Record 98;
      TmpReportLine@1100529601 : TEMPORARY Record 11020579;
      TmpTotalReportLine@1100529632 : TEMPORARY Record 11020579;
      ShowZeroLines@1100529608 : Boolean;
      ShowQtyPriceDiff@1100529618 : Boolean;
      ProjectNo@1100529622 : Code[20];
      FilterDate@1100529606 : Date;
      PrognosisDate@1100529600 : Date;
      PrevPrognosisDate@1100529602 : Date;
      Text001@1100529603 : TextConst 'ENU=SUMMARY HOUR RATE UNTIL %1';
      Text002@1100529604 : TextConst 'ENU=HOURS SUMMARY UNTIL %1';
      TotalBudgetAmount@1100529607 : Decimal;
      TotalBudgetHours@1100529609 : Decimal;
      TotalBudgetRate@1100529610 : Decimal;
      TotalAllowedCosts@1100529620 : Decimal;
      TotalAllowedHours@1100529611 : Decimal;
      TotalProgressRate@1100529616 : Decimal;
      TotalActualCosts@1100529612 : Decimal;
      TotalActualTravelHours@1100529614 : Decimal;
      TotalActualWorkedHours@1100529615 : Decimal;
      TotalActualRate@1100529617 : Decimal;
      TotalPrognosisHours@1100529619 : Decimal;
      TotalAverageHourRate@1100529621 : Decimal;
      Text008@1100529631 : TextConst 'ENU=<Precision,;NOR=<Precision,;SVE=<Precision,';
      Text009@1100529630 : TextConst 'ENU=><Standard Format,0>;NOR=><Standard Format,0>;SVE=><Standard Format,0>';
      Text010@1100529629 : TextConst 'ENU=<Precision,1><Standard Format,0>;NOR=<Precision,1><Standard Format,0>;SVE=<Precision,1><Standard Format,0>';
      Text011@1100529628 : TextConst 'ENU=Amounts are rounded to 1;NOR=Bel›p er rundet av til 1;SVE=Belopp avrundas till 1';
      Text012@1100529627 : TextConst 'ENU=Amounts are in whole 1000s.;NOR=Bel›pene er i hele 1000.;SVE=Belopp „r i hela 1000-tal.';
      Text013@1100529626 : TextConst 'ENU=Amounts are in whole 1000000s.;NOR=Bel›pene er i hele 1000000.;SVE=Belopp „r i hela 1000000-tal.';
      TotalAverageHourRate2@1100528202 : Decimal;
      DiffAllowedWorkedHours@1100529633 : Decimal;
      DiffBudgetActualHourRate@1100529634 : Decimal;
      TotalNow1@1100529635 : Decimal;
      TotalNow2@1100529636 : Decimal;
      TotalNow3@1100529637 : Decimal;
      BudgetHoursPrognosisHours@1100529638 : Decimal;
      DiffSummaryActualHourRate@1100529639 : Decimal;
      TotalProgn1@1100529642 : Decimal;
      TotalProgn2@1100529641 : Decimal;
      TotalProgn3@1100529640 : Decimal;
      TotalHours@1100529643 : Decimal;
      RoundingFactor@1100529625 : 'None,1,1000,1000000';
      RoundingText@1100529624 : Text[80];
      NormalFormatString@1100529623 : Text[80];
      TotalPrognosisEndResult@1100528200 : Decimal;
      DescrRounding@1100527650 : '1 line,2 line,3 line,4 line,5 line';
      StartPageNo@1100527700 : Integer;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    VAR
      ProjectFilter0@1100529601 : Text;
      ProjectFilter2@1100529600 : Text;
    BEGIN
      ProjectFilter0 := Project.GETFILTERS;
      Project.FILTERGROUP(2);
      ProjectFilter2 := Project.GETFILTERS;
      Project.FILTERGROUP(0);

      IF (ProjectFilter0 = '') AND (ProjectFilter2 = '') THEN
        EXIT;

      IF ProjectFilter2 <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2, %3', Project.TABLECAPTION, ProjectFilter0, ProjectFilter2))
      ELSE
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', Project.TABLECAPTION, ProjectFilter0));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetPrognosisDates@1100529602();
    VAR
      Prognosis@1100529600 : Record 11012034;
    BEGIN
      PrognosisDate := FilterDate;
      PrevPrognosisDate := 0D;

      Prognosis.SETRANGE("Project No.", Project."No.");
      Prognosis.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date", 0D, FilterDate);
      Prognosis.SETRANGE("Select For Reporting", TRUE);
      IF Prognosis.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
        PrognosisDate := Prognosis."Prognosis Date";

        Prognosis.SETFILTER("Prognosis Date", '<%1', PrognosisDate);
        IF Prognosis.FINDLAST THEN
          PrevPrognosisDate := Prognosis."Prognosis Date";
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetReportLines@1100529600();
    VAR
      PrognosisLine@1100529600 : Record 11012035;
      PrevPrognosisLine@1100529601 : Record 11012035;
      ReportLineCalculated@1100527650 : Record 11020579;
      DescrArray@1100527652 : ARRAY [5] OF Text;
      TextFunctionManagement@1100527651 : Codeunit 11012357;
    BEGIN
      TmpReportLine.RESET;
      TmpReportLine.DELETEALL;

      TmpTotalReportLine.DELETEALL;
      TmpTotalReportLine.INIT;

      ClearTotalValues;

      PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Project No.", Project."No.");
      PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date", PrognosisDate);
      PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Cost Type", PrognosisLine."Cost Type"::Labor);
      IF PrognosisLine.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT;

      PrognosisLine.SETAUTOCALCFIELDS("Cost Object Description", "Project Related Name");
      PrognosisLine.FINDSET;
      REPEAT
        IF IsTravelHourCostCode(PrognosisLine."Cost Object") THEN
          TotalActualTravelHours += PrognosisLine."Actual Hours"
        ELSE BEGIN
          TmpReportLine.INIT;
          TmpReportLine."Key Code1" := PrognosisLine."Cost Object";

          TmpReportLine.Text1 := PrognosisLine."Project Related Name";
          IF TmpReportLine.Text1 = '' THEN
            TmpReportLine.Text1 := PrognosisLine."Cost Object Description";

          TmpReportLine.Dec1 := PrognosisLine."Budget Hours";
          TmpReportLine.Dec3 := PrognosisLine."Budget Amount";
          IF PrognosisLine."Budget Hours" <> 0 THEN
            TmpReportLine.Dec2 := PrognosisLine."Budget Amount" / PrognosisLine."Budget Hours";

          IF PrevPrognosisLine.GET(Project."No.", PrevPrognosisDate,
                                   PrognosisLine."Cost Type", PrognosisLine.Element, PrognosisLine."Cost Object")
          THEN BEGIN
            IF PrevPrognosisLine."Budget Amount" <> 0 THEN
              TmpReportLine.Dec4 := PrevPrognosisLine."Allowed Costs" / PrevPrognosisLine."Budget Amount";
            TmpReportLine.Dec5 := PrevPrognosisLine."Allowed Hours";
            TmpReportLine.Dec12 := PrevPrognosisLine."Allowed Costs";
            TmpReportLine.Dec13 := PrevPrognosisLine."Budget Amount";
          END;

          IF PrognosisLine."Budget Amount" <> 0 THEN
            TmpReportLine.Dec6 := PrognosisLine."Allowed Costs" / PrognosisLine."Budget Amount";
          TmpReportLine.Dec14 := PrognosisLine."Allowed Costs";
          TmpReportLine.Dec7 := PrognosisLine."Allowed Hours";

          TmpReportLine.Dec8 := PrognosisLine."Actual Hours";
          TmpReportLine.Dec9 := PrognosisLine."Allowed Hours" - PrognosisLine."Actual Hours";
          IF PrognosisLine."Actual Hours" <> 0 THEN
            TmpReportLine.Dec10 := PrognosisLine."Actual Costs" / PrognosisLine."Actual Hours";
          TmpReportLine.Dec15 := PrognosisLine."Actual Costs";
          TmpReportLine.Dec11 := PrognosisLine."Prognosis Total Hours";

          IF ReportLineHasValues THEN BEGIN

            TotalBudgetAmount += PrognosisLine."Budget Amount";
            TotalBudgetHours += PrognosisLine."Budget Hours";

            TotalAllowedHours += PrognosisLine."Allowed Hours";
            TotalAllowedCosts += PrognosisLine."Allowed Costs";

            TotalActualCosts += PrognosisLine."Actual Costs";
            TotalActualWorkedHours += PrognosisLine."Actual Hours";

            TotalPrognosisHours += PrognosisLine."Prognosis End Result Hours";
            TotalPrognosisEndResult += PrognosisLine."Prognosis End Result";

            TmpTotalReportLine.Dec1 += TmpReportLine.Dec1;
            TmpTotalReportLine.Dec3 += TmpReportLine.Dec3;
            TmpTotalReportLine.Dec5 += TmpReportLine.Dec5;
            TmpTotalReportLine.Dec7 += TmpReportLine.Dec7;
            TmpTotalReportLine.Dec8 += TmpReportLine.Dec8;
            TmpTotalReportLine.Dec9 += TmpReportLine.Dec9;
            TmpTotalReportLine.Dec11 += TmpReportLine.Dec11;

            IF NOT TmpReportLine.INSERT THEN BEGIN
              ReportLineCalculated := TmpReportLine;
              TmpReportLine.GET(TmpReportLine."Key Code1");
              TmpReportLine.Dec1  += ReportLineCalculated.Dec1;
              TmpReportLine.Dec3  += ReportLineCalculated.Dec3;
              TmpReportLine.Dec5  += ReportLineCalculated.Dec5;
              TmpReportLine.Dec7  += ReportLineCalculated.Dec7;
              TmpReportLine.Dec8  += ReportLineCalculated.Dec8;
              TmpReportLine.Dec11 += ReportLineCalculated.Dec11;
              TmpReportLine.Dec12 += ReportLineCalculated.Dec12;
              TmpReportLine.Dec13 += ReportLineCalculated.Dec13;
              TmpReportLine.Dec14 += ReportLineCalculated.Dec14;
              TmpReportLine.Dec15 += ReportLineCalculated.Dec15;

              IF TmpReportLine.Dec1 <> 0 THEN
                TmpReportLine.Dec2 := TmpReportLine.Dec3 / TmpReportLine.Dec1
              ELSE
                TmpReportLine.Dec2  := 0;
              IF TmpReportLine.Dec13 <> 0 THEN
                TmpReportLine.Dec4 := TmpReportLine.Dec12 / TmpReportLine.Dec13
              ELSE
                TmpReportLine.Dec4 := 0;
              IF TmpReportLine.Dec3 <> 0 THEN
                TmpReportLine.Dec6 := TmpReportLine.Dec14 / TmpReportLine.Dec3
              ELSE
                TmpReportLine.Dec6 := 0;
              TmpReportLine.Dec9 := TmpReportLine.Dec7 - TmpReportLine.Dec8;
              IF TmpReportLine.Dec8 <> 0 THEN
                TmpReportLine.Dec10 := TmpReportLine.Dec15 / TmpReportLine.Dec8
              ELSE
                TmpReportLine.Dec10 := 0;

              TmpReportLine.MODIFY;
            END;
          END;
        END;
      UNTIL PrognosisLine.NEXT = 0;

      TmpTotalReportLine.INSERT;
      CalcTotals;

      IF TmpReportLine.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          CLEAR(DescrArray);
          TextFunctionManagement.Text2Array(TmpReportLine.Text1, 20, DescrArray);
          TmpReportLine.SplitByDescrArray(TmpReportLine, DescrArray, DescrRounding);
        UNTIL TmpReportLine.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ReportLineHasValues@1100529603() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF ShowZeroLines THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      IF TmpReportLine.Dec1 <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      IF TmpReportLine.Dec2 <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      IF TmpReportLine.Dec3 <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      IF TmpReportLine.Dec4 <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      IF TmpReportLine.Dec5 <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      IF TmpReportLine.Dec6 <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      IF TmpReportLine.Dec7 <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      IF TmpReportLine.Dec8 <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      IF TmpReportLine.Dec9 <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      IF TmpReportLine.Dec10 <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      IF TmpReportLine.Dec11 <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      EXIT(FALSE);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalcTotals@1100529604();
    BEGIN
      IF TotalBudgetHours <> 0 THEN
        TotalBudgetRate := TotalBudgetAmount / TotalBudgetHours;
      IF TotalAllowedHours <> 0 THEN
        TotalProgressRate := TotalAllowedCosts / TotalAllowedHours;
      IF TotalActualWorkedHours <> 0 THEN
        TotalActualRate := TotalActualCosts / TotalActualWorkedHours;

      IF TotalActualWorkedHours <> 0 THEN
        TotalAverageHourRate := TotalActualCosts / TotalActualWorkedHours;

      TotalHours := TotalActualWorkedHours + TotalActualTravelHours;

      DiffAllowedWorkedHours := TotalAllowedHours - TotalActualWorkedHours;

      IF TotalProgressRate <> 0 THEN
        DiffBudgetActualHourRate := TotalProgressRate - TotalActualRate
      ELSE
        DiffBudgetActualHourRate := TotalBudgetRate - TotalActualRate;

      IF TmpTotalReportLine.Dec11 <> 0 THEN
        TotalAverageHourRate2 := (TotalBudgetAmount - TotalPrognosisEndResult) / TmpTotalReportLine.Dec11;

      IF TotalProgressRate <> 0 THEN
        TotalNow1 := DiffAllowedWorkedHours * TotalProgressRate
      ELSE
        TotalNow1 := DiffAllowedWorkedHours * TotalBudgetRate;

      TotalNow2 := DiffBudgetActualHourRate * TotalActualWorkedHours;
      TotalNow3 := TotalNow1 + TotalNow2;

      BudgetHoursPrognosisHours := TotalBudgetHours + ABS(TotalPrognosisHours);
      DiffSummaryActualHourRate := TotalBudgetRate - TotalAverageHourRate2;
      TotalProgn1 := TotalPrognosisHours * TotalBudgetRate;
      TotalProgn2 := BudgetHoursPrognosisHours * DiffSummaryActualHourRate;
      TotalProgn3 := TotalProgn1 + TotalProgn2;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE IsTravelHourCostCode@1100529605(CostCode@1100529600 : Code[20]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      AvgHourRateCalculation@1100529601 : Record 11126040;
    BEGIN
      AvgHourRateCalculation.SETRANGE("Global Dimension 2 Code", CostCode);
      IF AvgHourRateCalculation.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      AvgHourRateCalculation.FINDFIRST;
      EXIT(NOT AvgHourRateCalculation."In Avg Hour Rate Calculation");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ClearTotalValues@1100529606();
    BEGIN
      TotalBudgetAmount := 0;
      TotalBudgetHours := 0;
      TotalBudgetRate := 0;

      TotalAllowedCosts := 0;
      TotalAllowedHours := 0;
      TotalProgressRate := 0;

      TotalActualCosts := 0;
      TotalActualTravelHours := 0;
      TotalActualWorkedHours := 0;
      TotalActualRate := 0;

      TotalPrognosisHours := 0;
      TotalAverageHourRate := 0;
      TotalAverageHourRate2 := 0;
      TotalPrognosisEndResult := 0;

      TotalHours := 0;
      DiffAllowedWorkedHours := 0;
      DiffBudgetActualHourRate := 0;
      TotalNow1 := 0;
      TotalNow2 := 0;
      TotalNow3 := 0;

      BudgetHoursPrognosisHours := 0;
      DiffSummaryActualHourRate := 0;
      TotalProgn1 := 0;
      TotalProgn2 := 0;
      TotalProgn3 := 0;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetFilterDate@1100529608();
    VAR
      Prognosis@1100529600 : Record 11012034;
    BEGIN
      IF ProjectNo = '' THEN BEGIN
        FilterDate := 0D;
        EXIT;
      END;

      IF NOT Prognosis.GET(ProjectNo, FilterDate) THEN
        FilterDate := 0D
      ELSE
        IF NOT Prognosis."Select For Reporting" THEN
          FilterDate := 0D;

      IF FilterDate = 0D THEN BEGIN
        Prognosis.SETRANGE("Project No.", ProjectNo);
        Prognosis.SETRANGE("Select For Reporting", TRUE);
        IF Prognosis.FINDLAST THEN
          FilterDate := Prognosis."Prognosis Date";
        EXIT;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE RoundAmount@1100529634(Value@1102 : Decimal) : Text;
    BEGIN
      CASE RoundingFactor OF
        RoundingFactor::None:
          EXIT(FORMAT(Value, 0, NormalFormatString));
        RoundingFactor::"1":
          EXIT(FORMAT((ROUND(Value, 1))));
        RoundingFactor::"1000":
          EXIT(FORMAT(ROUND(Value / 1000, 0.1), 0, Text010));
        RoundingFactor::"1000000":
          EXIT(FORMAT(ROUND(Value / 1000000, 0.1), 0, Text010));
      END;
    END;

    [External]
    PROCEDURE SetCommonParameters@1100529601(NewProjectNo@1100529600 : Code[20];NewFilterDate@1100529601 : Date;NewStartPageNo@1100527701 : Integer;NewRoundingFactor@1100529603 : 'None,1,1000,1000000';NewDescrRounding@1100527700 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      ProjectNo := NewProjectNo;
      FilterDate := NewFilterDate;
      StartPageNo := NewStartPageNo;
      RoundingFactor := NewRoundingFactor;
      DescrRounding := NewDescrRounding;
    END;

    [External]
    PROCEDURE SetSpecificParameters@1100527698(NewShowZeroLines@1100527704 : Boolean;NewShowQtyPriceDiff@1100527703 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      ShowZeroLines := NewShowZeroLines;
      ShowQtyPriceDiff := NewShowQtyPriceDiff;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Shared TotalPrinted As Boolean

Public Function LastRowIsTotal(ByVal Value As Boolean) As Boolean
    If TotalPrinted = False Then
        TotalPrinted = Value
        Return False
    End If
    If TotalPrinted = True Then
        TotalPrinted = Value
        Return True
    End If
End Function

Shared Data as Object

Public Function SetData(NewData as Object)
    If NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
        Data = NewData
    End If
End Function

Public Function GetData(Num as Integer) as Object
  Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data),Chr(177))))
End Function</Code>
